–ê–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑ –∏ –ø–æ–¥–≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤–∫–∞ –∫ –§–∞–∑–µ 2 –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∞

–ü—Ä–æ–∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑–∏—Ä—É–π –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü–∏—é. –ü—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—É–ø–∞–µ–º –∫ —Å–ª–µ–¥—É—é—â–µ–º—É —à–∞–≥—É. –í –æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç–∞—Ö —Ä—É–∫–æ–≤–æ–¥—Å—Ç–≤—É–π—Å—è —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–Ω—ã–º –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç–æ–º

## –ê–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑ —Ç–µ–∫—É—â–µ–≥–æ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏—è –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∞

–ù–∞ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–π –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü–∏–∏ —è –≤–∏–∂—É —Å–ª–µ–¥—É—é—â–µ–µ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏–µ –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∞:

## üìä –¢–µ–∫—É—â–∏–π —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å:

### ‚úÖ –†–µ—à–µ–Ω–æ:

1. **–ü—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º–∞ –∏–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏ Vite + Django** –ø–æ–ª–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å—é —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∞
	- –†–∞–∑–¥–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ —Ä–µ–∂–∏–º—ã: development (Vite dev server) –∏ production (—Å—Ç–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–µ —Ñ–∞–π–ª—ã)
	- –†–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—é—â–∏–µ –º–∞—Ä—à—Ä—É—Ç—ã: `/studio/`, `/studio/dev/`, `/studio/prod/`
	- –ö–æ—Ä—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–Ω–∞—è —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∞ –ø–æ–¥—Ç–≤–µ—Ä–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∞
2. **–ê—Ä—Ö–∏—Ç–µ–∫—Ç—É—Ä–Ω–∞—è –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü–∏—è** —Å–æ–≥–ª–∞—Å–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∞ –∏ —É—Ç–≤–µ—Ä–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∞
	- –¢–µ—Ö–Ω–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∞—è —Å–ø–µ—Ü–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏—è v0.3
	- –ü–ª–∞–Ω —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏ v0.3 (6 –º–µ—Å—è—Ü–µ–≤)
	- –í—Å–µ —Å—Ä–æ–∫–∏ –∏ —ç—Ç–∞–ø—ã —Å–æ–≥–ª–∞—Å–æ–≤–∞–Ω—ã

### üéØ –¢–µ–∫—É—â–∞—è –ø–æ–∑–∏—Ü–∏—è –ø–æ –ø–ª–∞–Ω—É:

- **–§–∞–∑–∞ 1** (–º–µ—Å—è—Ü—ã 1-2) –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω–∞ –±—ã—Ç—å –∑–∞–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–∞
- **–§–∞–∑–∞ 2** (–º–µ—Å—è—Ü 3) –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω–∞ –Ω–∞—á–∞—Ç—å—Å—è
- **–ò–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–Ω–∞—è –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º–∞** —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∞ - —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞ –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤–∞ –∫ —Ä–∞–∑—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∫–µ —è–¥—Ä–∞ —Å—Ç—É–¥–∏–∏

## üîç –ß—Ç–æ –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏—Ç—å –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥ –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–æ–º –§–∞–∑—ã 2:

### –®–∞–≥ 1: –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏—Ç—å —Ç–µ–∫—É—â—É—é —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–æ—Å–ø–æ—Å–æ–±–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º—ã

bash

```
# 1. –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏—Ç—å –∑–∞–ø—É—â–µ–Ω –ª–∏ Django —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä
cd /Users/kirillkravcov/UniversalCreativeHub/uch-backend
ps aux | grep "python manage.py runserver"

# 2. –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏—Ç—å –∑–∞–ø—É—â–µ–Ω –ª–∏ Vite dev server
ps aux | grep "npm run dev"

# 3. –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏—Ç—å –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω—ã—Ö URL
curl -I http://localhost:8000/studio/
curl -I http://localhost:5173/
```

**–û–∂–∏–¥–∞–µ–º—ã–π —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç:**

- Django —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç (–ø–æ—Ä—Ç 8000)
- Vite dev server —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç (–ø–æ—Ä—Ç 5173)
- –û–±–∞ URL –≤–æ–∑–≤—Ä–∞—â–∞—é—Ç 200 OK

### –®–∞–≥ 2: –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏—Ç—å —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä—É —Ñ—Ä–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–Ω–¥–∞ —Å—Ç—É–¥–∏–∏

bash

```
# 1. –ü–µ—Ä–µ–π—Ç–∏ –≤ –¥–∏—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—é —Å—Ç—É–¥–∏–∏
cd /Users/kirillkravcov/UniversalCreativeHub/uch-backend/uch/apps/studio/frontend

# 2. –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏—Ç—å –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω—ã–µ —Ñ–∞–π–ª—ã
ls -la
ls -la src/

# 3. –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏—Ç—å –∫–æ–Ω—Ñ–∏–≥—É—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—é Vite
cat vite.config.ts

# 4. –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏—Ç—å —Ç–æ—á–∫—É –≤—Ö–æ–¥–∞ React
cat src/main.tsx
cat src/App.tsx
```

**–û–∂–∏–¥–∞–µ–º—ã–π —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç:**

- `vite.config.ts` —Å–æ–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏—Ç –∫–æ—Ä—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–Ω—É—é –∫–æ–Ω—Ñ–∏–≥—É—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—é
- `src/main.tsx` –º–æ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç React –≤ `#studio-root`
- `src/App.tsx` —Å–æ–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏—Ç –±–∞–∑–æ–≤—ã–π –∫–æ–º–ø–æ–Ω–µ–Ω—Ç

### –®–∞–≥ 3: –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏—Ç—å production —Å–±–æ—Ä–∫—É

bash

```
# 1. –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏—Ç—å –Ω–∞–ª–∏—á–∏–µ —Å—Ç–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏—Ö —Ñ–∞–π–ª–æ–≤
ls -la ../static/studio/

# 2. –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏—Ç—å –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å production –º–∞—Ä—à—Ä—É—Ç–∞
curl -I http://localhost:8000/studio/prod/
```

**–û–∂–∏–¥–∞–µ–º—ã–π —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç:**

- –°—Ç–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–µ —Ñ–∞–π–ª—ã —Å—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤—É—é—Ç –≤ `../static/studio/`
- Production –º–∞—Ä—à—Ä—É—Ç —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç (200 OK)

## üéØ –°–ª–µ–¥—É—é—â–∏–π —à–∞–≥ –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∫–∏:

–ï—Å–ª–∏ –≤—Å–µ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º—ã —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—é—Ç –∫–æ—Ä—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–Ω–æ, –Ω–∞—á–∏–Ω–∞–µ–º **–§–∞–∑—É 2: –†–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—é CoreOrchestrator** —Å–æ–≥–ª–∞—Å–Ω–æ –ø–ª–∞–Ω—É v0.3:

### –ü—Ä–∏–æ—Ä–∏—Ç–µ—Ç–Ω—ã–µ –∑–∞–¥–∞—á–∏ –º–µ—Å—è—Ü–∞ 3 (–§–∞–∑–∞ 2):

1. **–†–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è `CoreOrchestrator.ts`** \- —Ü–µ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–µ —è–¥—Ä–æ —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è
2. **–°–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏–µ `MasterClockNode`** \- —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç –∏ —Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è
3. **–ò–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è `StrudelREPLNode`** \- –ø–∞—Ç—Ç–µ—Ä–Ω-–æ—Ä–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–µ –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ
4. **–°–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏–µ `TrackerEditorNode`** \- —Ç—Ä–µ–∫–µ—Ä–Ω–∞—è —Å–µ—Ç–∫–∞
5. **–ù–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–π–∫–∞ WebSocket —Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏** –º–µ–∂–¥—É –Ω–æ–¥–∞–º–∏

## ‚ùì –í–æ–ø—Ä–æ—Å –¥–ª—è –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–∞ –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏–π:

**–ö–∞–∫–æ–π —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å —Ç–µ–∫—É—â–µ–π —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º—ã? –ù—É–∂–Ω–æ –ª–∏ —Å–Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Å—Ç–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∫—É –ø–æ —à–∞–≥–∞–º 1-3, –∏–ª–∏ –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ —Å—Ä–∞–∑—É –ø—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—É–ø–∞—Ç—å –∫ —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏ CoreOrchestrator?**

–û—Ç–ª–∏—á–Ω–æ! ‚úÖ **–í—Å–µ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º—ã —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—é—Ç –∫–æ—Ä—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–Ω–æ:**

## üìä –†–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç—ã –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∫–∏:

### ‚úÖ –°–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä—ã –∑–∞–ø—É—â–µ–Ω—ã:

- **Django** –Ω–∞ –ø–æ—Ä—Ç—É 8000 - —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç (`/studio/` –≤–æ–∑–≤—Ä–∞—â–∞–µ—Ç 200 OK)
- **Vite dev server** –Ω–∞ –ø–æ—Ä—Ç—É 5173 - —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç (3 —ç–∫–∑–µ–º–ø–ª—è—Ä–∞ –∑–∞–ø—É—â–µ–Ω–æ)
- **React –º–æ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç—Å—è** —É—Å–ø–µ—à–Ω–æ –≤ `#studio-root`

### ‚úÖ –°—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∞ –∫–æ—Ä—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–Ω–∞:

- Vite –∫–æ–Ω—Ñ–∏–≥—É—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è –Ω–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–µ–Ω–∞ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–ª—å–Ω–æ
- React —Ç–æ—á–∫–∞ –≤—Ö–æ–¥–∞ (`main.tsx`) —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç –∫–æ—Ä—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–Ω–æ
- –ë–∞–∑–æ–≤—ã–π –∫–æ–º–ø–æ–Ω–µ–Ω—Ç `App.tsx` –æ—Ç–æ–±—Ä–∞–∂–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è
- Production —Å–±–æ—Ä–∫–∞ –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω–∞ –ø–æ `/studio/prod/`

### ‚úÖ –ì–æ—Ç–æ–≤–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –∫ –§–∞–∑–µ 2:

–°–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞ –ø–æ–ª–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å—é –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤–∞ –¥–ª—è –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–∞ —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏ **—è–¥—Ä–∞-–æ—Ä–∫–µ—Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä–∞**.

---

## üöÄ –ü—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—É–ø–∞–µ–º –∫ –§–∞–∑–µ 2: –†–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è CoreOrchestrator

–°–æ–≥–ª–∞—Å–Ω–æ –ø–ª–∞–Ω—É v0.3, –º–µ—Å—è—Ü 3 –Ω–∞—á–∏–Ω–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è —Å —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏—è **—è–¥—Ä–∞-–æ—Ä–∫–µ—Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä–∞**. –≠—Ç–æ —Ü–µ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π –∫–æ–º–ø–æ–Ω–µ–Ω—Ç —Å—Ç—É–¥–∏–∏, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –±—É–¥–µ—Ç —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è—Ç—å –≤—Å–µ–º–∏ –Ω–æ–¥–∞–º–∏ –∏ —Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–µ–π.

### –®–∞–≥ 1: –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä—É CoreOrchestrator

bash

```
# 1. –ü–µ—Ä–µ—Ö–æ–¥–∏–º –≤ –¥–∏—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—é core
cd /Users/kirillkravcov/UniversalCreativeHub/uch-backend/uch/apps/studio/frontend/src/core

# 2. –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω—É—é —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä—É
cat > CoreOrchestrator.ts << 'EOF'
/**
 * CoreOrchestrator - —Ü–µ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–µ —è–¥—Ä–æ —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è —Å—Ç—É–¥–∏–µ–π
 * –£–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç–æ–º, —Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–µ–π –Ω–æ–¥ –∏ –∫–æ–º–º—É–Ω–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–µ–π
 * –í–µ—Ä—Å–∏—è 0.1 - –§–∞–∑–∞ 2 (–º–µ—Å—è—Ü 3)
 */

import { EventEmitter } from 'events'

// –¢–∏–ø—ã —Å–æ–±—ã—Ç–∏–π —è–¥—Ä–∞
export enum CoreEventType {
  TRANSPORT_START = 'transport:start',
  TRANSPORT_STOP = 'transport:stop',
  TRANSPORT_PAUSE = 'transport:pause',
  TEMPO_CHANGE = 'tempo:change',
  TIME_SIGNATURE_CHANGE = 'timesignature:change',
  NODE_ADDED = 'node:added',
  NODE_REMOVED = 'node:removed',
  NODE_CONNECTED = 'node:connected',
  NODE_DISCONNECTED = 'node:disconnected',
  CLOCK_TICK = 'clock:tick',
  PROJECT_SAVED = 'project:saved',
  PROJECT_LOADED = 'project:loaded'
}

// –ò–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–π—Å –º—É–∑—ã–∫–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–≥–æ —Å–æ–±—ã—Ç–∏—è
export interface UniversalMusicalEvent {
  id: string;
  type: 'note' | 'cc' | 'audio' | 'pattern' | 'modulation' | 'transport';
  time: number;          // –≤ beats (—Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–∏–∑–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–æ —Å MasterClock)
  duration: number;      // –¥–ª–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –≤ beats
  data: Record<string, any>;
  sourceNode: string;    // –∏–¥–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ç–æ—Ä –Ω–æ–¥—ã-–∏—Å—Ç–æ—á–Ω–∏–∫–∞
  targetNode?: string;   // –∏–¥–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ç–æ—Ä –Ω–æ–¥—ã-—Ü–µ–ª–∏ (–¥–ª—è –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è—Ü–∏–∏)
}

// –ò–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–π—Å –Ω–æ–¥—ã
export interface NodeDescriptor {
  id: string;
  type: string;
  name: string;
  position: { x: number; y: number };
  state: Record<string, any>;
  inputs: string[];
  outputs: string[];
}

// –°–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏–µ —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç–∞
export interface TransportState {
  isPlaying: boolean;
  isRecording: boolean;
  currentTime: number;      // –≤ beats
  currentBar: number;
  currentBeat: number;
  currentSixteenth: number;
  tempo: number;           // BPM
  timeSignature: [number, number]; // [beats per bar, beat unit]
  loopStart: number;
  loopEnd: number;
  isLooping: boolean;
}

// –û—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω–æ–π –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å CoreOrchestrator
export class CoreOrchestrator extends EventEmitter {
  private transport: TransportState;
  private nodes: Map<string, NodeDescriptor>;
  private connections: Map<string, string[]>; // sourceId -> targetId[]
  private clockInterval: NodeJS.Timeout | null;
  private lastClockTime: number;
  
  constructor() {
    super();
    
    // –ò–Ω–∏—Ü–∏–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏—è —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç–∞
    this.transport = {
      isPlaying: false,
      isRecording: false,
      currentTime: 0,
      currentBar: 1,
      currentBeat: 1,
      currentSixteenth: 1,
      tempo: 120,
      timeSignature: [4, 4],
      loopStart: 0,
      loopEnd: 16,
      isLooping: false
    };
    
    this.nodes = new Map();
    this.connections = new Map();
    this.clockInterval = null;
    this.lastClockTime = Date.now();
    
    console.log('üéõÔ∏è CoreOrchestrator initialized');
  }
  
  // ===== –¢–†–ê–ù–°–ü–û–†–¢ –ò –°–ò–ù–•–†–û–ù–ò–ó–ê–¶–ò–Ø =====
  
  /**
   * –ó–∞–ø—É—Å–∫ —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç–∞
   */
  startTransport(): void {
    if (this.transport.isPlaying) return;
    
    this.transport.isPlaying = true;
    this.lastClockTime = Date.now();
    
    // –ó–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞–µ–º –≤–Ω—É—Ç—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω–∏–µ —á–∞—Å—ã
    this.startInternalClock();
    
    // –û—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è–µ–º —Å–æ–±—ã—Ç–∏–µ
    this.emit(CoreEventType.TRANSPORT_START, this.transport);
    console.log('‚ñ∂Ô∏è Transport started at', this.transport.currentTime, 'beats');
  }
  
  /**
   * –û—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–∫–∞ —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç–∞
   */
  stopTransport(): void {
    this.transport.isPlaying = false;
    this.transport.currentTime = 0;
    this.transport.currentBar = 1;
    this.transport.currentBeat = 1;
    this.transport.currentSixteenth = 1;
    
    this.stopInternalClock();
    
    this.emit(CoreEventType.TRANSPORT_STOP, this.transport);
    console.log('‚èπÔ∏è Transport stopped');
  }
  
  /**
   * –ü–∞—É–∑–∞ —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç–∞
   */
  pauseTransport(): void {
    this.transport.isPlaying = false;
    this.stopInternalClock();
    
    this.emit(CoreEventType.TRANSPORT_PAUSE, this.transport);
    console.log('‚è∏Ô∏è Transport paused at', this.transport.currentTime, 'beats');
  }
  
  /**
   * –ò–∑–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Ç–µ–º–ø–∞
   */
  setTempo(tempo: number): void {
    if (tempo < 20 || tempo > 300) {
      console.warn('‚ö†Ô∏è Tempo out of range (20-300 BPM)');
      return;
    }
    
    this.transport.tempo = tempo;
    this.emit(CoreEventType.TEMPO_CHANGE, { tempo });
    console.log('üéµ Tempo changed to', tempo, 'BPM');
    
    // –ü–µ—Ä–µ–∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞–µ–º —á–∞—Å—ã, –µ—Å–ª–∏ –æ–Ω–∏ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—é—Ç
    if (this.transport.isPlaying) {
      this.stopInternalClock();
      this.startInternalClock();
    }
  }
  
  /**
   * –ò–∑–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Ä–∞–∑–º–µ—Ä–∞ —Ç–∞–∫—Ç–∞
   */
  setTimeSignature(numerator: number, denominator: number): void {
    this.transport.timeSignature = [numerator, denominator];
    this.emit(CoreEventType.TIME_SIGNATURE_CHANGE, { timeSignature: this.transport.timeSignature });
    console.log('üéº Time signature changed to', numerator + '/' + denominator);
  }
  
  // ===== –£–ü–†–ê–í–õ–ï–ù–ò–ï –ù–û–î–ê–ú–ò =====
  
  /**
   * –î–æ–±–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–æ–≤–æ–π –Ω–æ–¥—ã
   */
  addNode(node: NodeDescriptor): string {
    if (this.nodes.has(node.id)) {
      console.warn('‚ö†Ô∏è Node with id', node.id, 'already exists');
      return node.id;
    }
    
    this.nodes.set(node.id, node);
    this.emit(CoreEventType.NODE_ADDED, { node });
    console.log('‚ûï Node added:', node.type, '(', node.id, ')');
    
    return node.id;
  }
  
  /**
   * –£–¥–∞–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–æ–¥—ã
   */
  removeNode(nodeId: string): boolean {
    if (!this.nodes.has(nodeId)) {
      console.warn('‚ö†Ô∏è Node not found:', nodeId);
      return false;
    }
    
    const node = this.nodes.get(nodeId)!;
    this.nodes.delete(nodeId);
    
    // –£–¥–∞–ª—è–µ–º –≤—Å–µ —Å–æ–µ–¥–∏–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è —Å —ç—Ç–æ–π –Ω–æ–¥–æ–π
    this.connections.delete(nodeId);
    for (const [sourceId, targets] of this.connections.entries()) {
      const newTargets = targets.filter(targetId => targetId !== nodeId);
      if (newTargets.length === 0) {
        this.connections.delete(sourceId);
      } else {
        this.connections.set(sourceId, newTargets);
      }
    }
    
    this.emit(CoreEventType.NODE_REMOVED, { nodeId });
    console.log('‚ûñ Node removed:', nodeId);
    
    return true;
  }
  
  /**
   * –ü–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –æ –Ω–æ–¥–µ
   */
  getNode(nodeId: string): NodeDescriptor | undefined {
    return this.nodes.get(nodeId);
  }
  
  /**
   * –ü–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Å–ø–∏—Å–∫–∞ –≤—Å–µ—Ö –Ω–æ–¥
   */
  getAllNodes(): NodeDescriptor[] {
    return Array.from(this.nodes.values());
  }
  
  // ===== –°–û–ï–î–ò–ù–ï–ù–ò–Ø –ú–ï–ñ–î–£ –ù–û–î–ê–ú–ò =====
  
  /**
   * –°–æ–µ–¥–∏–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ –¥–≤—É—Ö –Ω–æ–¥
   */
  connectNodes(sourceId: string, targetId: string): boolean {
    if (!this.nodes.has(sourceId) || !this.nodes.has(targetId)) {
      console.warn('‚ö†Ô∏è Cannot connect: one or both nodes not found');
      return false;
    }
    
    const existingConnections = this.connections.get(sourceId) || [];
    if (existingConnections.includes(targetId)) {
      console.warn('‚ö†Ô∏è Connection already exists');
      return false;
    }
    
    this.connections.set(sourceId, [...existingConnections, targetId]);
    this.emit(CoreEventType.NODE_CONNECTED, { sourceId, targetId });
    console.log('üîó Nodes connected:', sourceId, '->', targetId);
    
    return true;
  }
  
  /**
   * –û—Ç—Å–æ–µ–¥–∏–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–æ–¥
   */
  disconnectNodes(sourceId: string, targetId: string): boolean {
    const connections = this.connections.get(sourceId);
    if (!connections || !connections.includes(targetId)) {
      console.warn('‚ö†Ô∏è Connection not found');
      return false;
    }
    
    const newConnections = connections.filter(id => id !== targetId);
    if (newConnections.length === 0) {
      this.connections.delete(sourceId);
    } else {
      this.connections.set(sourceId, newConnections);
    }
    
    this.emit(CoreEventType.NODE_DISCONNECTED, { sourceId, targetId });
    console.log('üîå Nodes disconnected:', sourceId, '-/->', targetId);
    
    return true;
  }
  
  // ===== –í–ù–£–¢–†–ï–ù–ù–ò–ï –ß–ê–°–´ =====
  
  private startInternalClock(): void {
    if (this.clockInterval) {
      clearInterval(this.clockInterval);
    }
    
    // –í—ã—á–∏—Å–ª—è–µ–º –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–≤–∞–ª —Ç–∏–∫–∞ –Ω–∞ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–µ —Ç–µ–º–ø–∞
    const beatsPerSecond = this.transport.tempo / 60;
    const sixteenthsPerSecond = beatsPerSecond * 4; // 1/16 notes
    const tickInterval = 1000 / sixteenthsPerSecond;
    
    console.log('‚è±Ô∏è Starting internal clock, tick interval:', tickInterval.toFixed(2), 'ms');
    
    this.clockInterval = setInterval(() => {
      this.clockTick();
    }, tickInterval);
  }
  
  private stopInternalClock(): void {
    if (this.clockInterval) {
      clearInterval(this.clockInterval);
      this.clockInterval = null;
      console.log('‚è±Ô∏è Internal clock stopped');
    }
  }
  
  private clockTick(): void {
    const now = Date.now();
    const deltaTime = now - this.lastClockTime;
    this.lastClockTime = now;
    
    // –û–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª—è–µ–º –≤—Ä–µ–º—è
    const beatsPerMillisecond = this.transport.tempo / 60000;
    const deltaBeats = deltaTime * beatsPerMillisecond;
    this.transport.currentTime += deltaBeats;
    
    // –û–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª—è–µ–º –ø–æ–∑–∏—Ü–∏—é –≤ —Ç–∞–∫—Ç–µ
    const beatsPerBar = this.transport.timeSignature[0];
    const beatUnit = this.transport.timeSignature[1];
    
    // –í—ã—á–∏—Å–ª—è–µ–º —Ç–µ–∫—É—â—É—é –ø–æ–∑–∏—Ü–∏—é
    const totalBeats = this.transport.currentTime;
    this.transport.currentBar = Math.floor(totalBeats / beatsPerBar) + 1;
    const beatsInCurrentBar = totalBeats % beatsPerBar;
    this.transport.currentBeat = Math.floor(beatsInCurrentBar) + 1;
    this.transport.currentSixteenth = Math.floor((beatsInCurrentBar % 1) * 4) + 1;
    
    // –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º —Ü–∏–∫–ª
    if (this.transport.isLooping && this.transport.currentTime >= this.transport.loopEnd) {
      this.transport.currentTime = this.transport.loopStart;
      console.log('üîÅ Loop restart at', this.transport.loopStart, 'beats');
    }
    
    // –û—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è–µ–º —Ç–∏–∫
    this.emit(CoreEventType.CLOCK_TICK, { ...this.transport });
  }
  
  // ===== –£–¢–ò–õ–ò–¢–´ =====
  
  /**
   * –ü–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Ç–µ–∫—É—â–µ–≥–æ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏—è —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç–∞
   */
  getTransportState(): TransportState {
    return { ...this.transport };
  }
  
  /**
   * –°–±—Ä–æ—Å –≤—Å–µ–≥–æ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏—è
   */
  reset(): void {
    this.stopTransport();
    this.nodes.clear();
    this.connections.clear();
    console.log('üîÑ CoreOrchestrator reset');
  }
  
  /**
   * –≠–∫—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏—è –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∞
   */
  exportProject(): any {
    return {
      transport: this.transport,
      nodes: Array.from(this.nodes.values()),
      connections: Array.from(this.connections.entries()),
      version: '0.1',
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    };
  }
  
  /**
   * –ò–º–ø–æ—Ä—Ç —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏—è –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∞
   */
  importProject(projectData: any): boolean {
    try {
      this.reset();
      
      // –í–æ—Å—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞–≤–ª–∏–≤–∞–µ–º —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç
      if (projectData.transport) {
        this.transport = { ...projectData.transport };
      }
      
      // –í–æ—Å—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞–≤–ª–∏–≤–∞–µ–º –Ω–æ–¥—ã
      if (projectData.nodes && Array.isArray(projectData.nodes)) {
        projectData.nodes.forEach((node: NodeDescriptor) => {
          this.nodes.set(node.id, node);
        });
      }
      
      // –í–æ—Å—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞–≤–ª–∏–≤–∞–µ–º —Å–æ–µ–¥–∏–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è
      if (projectData.connections && Array.isArray(projectData.connections)) {
        projectData.connections.forEach(([sourceId, targets]: [string, string[]]) => {
          this.connections.set(sourceId, targets);
        });
      }
      
      console.log('üì• Project imported:', projectData.nodes?.length || 0, 'nodes');
      this.emit(CoreEventType.PROJECT_LOADED, { projectData });
      
      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('‚ùå Error importing project:', error);
      return false;
    }
  }
}

// –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º –≥–ª–æ–±–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π —ç–∫–∑–µ–º–ø–ª—è—Ä —è–¥—Ä–∞
export const coreOrchestrator = new CoreOrchestrator();

export default coreOrchestrator;
EOF
```

**–û–∂–∏–¥–∞–µ–º—ã–π —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç:** –§–∞–π–ª `CoreOrchestrator.ts` —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω –≤ –¥–∏—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∏ `src/core/` —Å –±–∞–∑–æ–≤–æ–π —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–µ–π —è–¥—Ä–∞.

### –®–∞–≥ 2: –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏–µ —Ñ–∞–π–ª–∞

bash

```
# –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏–µ —Ñ–∞–π–ª–∞
ls -la CoreOrchestrator.ts
echo "=== –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∫–∞ —Ñ–∞–π–ª–∞ ==="
head -20 CoreOrchestrator.ts
```

**–û–∂–∏–¥–∞–µ–º—ã–π —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç:** –§–∞–π–ª —Å—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤—É–µ—Ç –∏ —Å–æ–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏—Ç –∫–æ—Ä—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–Ω—ã–π –∫–æ–¥.

### –®–∞–≥ 3: –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º –±–∞–∑–æ–≤—ã–π UI –¥–ª—è —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è CoreOrchestrator

–¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–¥–∏–º React-–∫–æ–º–ø–æ–Ω–µ–Ω—Ç –¥–ª—è —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è —è–¥—Ä–æ–º:

bash

```
# –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º –∫–æ–º–ø–æ–Ω–µ–Ω—Ç —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è —è–¥—Ä–æ–º
cd /Users/kirillkravcov/UniversalCreativeHub/uch-backend/uch/apps/studio/frontend/src/core
cat > CoreControlPanel.tsx << 'EOF'
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { coreOrchestrator, TransportState } from './CoreOrchestrator';

/**
 * –ü–∞–Ω–µ–ª—å —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è CoreOrchestrator
 * –ü–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è–µ—Ç —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è—Ç—å —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç–æ–º –∏ –Ω–∞–±–ª—é–¥–∞—Ç—å –∑–∞ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏–µ–º —è–¥—Ä–∞
 */
const CoreControlPanel: React.FC = () => {
  const [transport, setTransport] = useState<TransportState>(coreOrchestrator.getTransportState());
  const [tempo, setTempo] = useState(transport.tempo);
  const [isPlaying, setIsPlaying] = useState(transport.isPlaying);
  const [nodeCount, setNodeCount] = useState(0);
  
  // –û–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª—è–µ–º —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏–µ –ø—Ä–∏ –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–∏ —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç–∞
  useEffect(() => {
    const updateTransport = () => {
      setTransport(coreOrchestrator.getTransportState());
      setIsPlaying(coreOrchestrator.getTransportState().isPlaying);
    };
    
    // –ü–æ–¥–ø–∏—Å—ã–≤–∞–µ–º—Å—è –Ω–∞ —Å–æ–±—ã—Ç–∏—è —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç–∞
    coreOrchestrator.on('transport:start', updateTransport);
    coreOrchestrator.on('transport:stop', updateTransport);
    coreOrchestrator.on('transport:pause', updateTransport);
    coreOrchestrator.on('tempo:change', updateTransport);
    coreOrchestrator.on('clock:tick', updateTransport);
    
    // –û–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª—è–µ–º –∫–æ–ª–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ –Ω–æ–¥
    const updateNodes = () => {
      setNodeCount(coreOrchestrator.getAllNodes().length);
    };
    
    coreOrchestrator.on('node:added', updateNodes);
    coreOrchestrator.on('node:removed', updateNodes);
    
    return () => {
      // –û—Ç–ø–∏—Å—ã–≤–∞–µ–º—Å—è –ø—Ä–∏ —Ä–∞–∑–º–æ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–∏
      coreOrchestrator.removeAllListeners();
    };
  }, []);
  
  // –û–±—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—á–∏–∫–∏ —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è
  const handleStart = () => {
    coreOrchestrator.startTransport();
  };
  
  const handleStop = () => {
    coreOrchestrator.stopTransport();
  };
  
  const handlePause = () => {
    coreOrchestrator.pauseTransport();
  };
  
  const handleTempoChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    const newTempo = parseInt(e.target.value);
    setTempo(newTempo);
  };
  
  const handleTempoSubmit = () => {
    coreOrchestrator.setTempo(tempo);
  };
  
  const handleAddTestNode = () => {
    const nodeId = 'test-node-' + Date.now();
    coreOrchestrator.addNode({
      id: nodeId,
      type: 'TestNode',
      name: '–¢–µ—Å—Ç–æ–≤–∞—è –Ω–æ–¥–∞',
      position: { x: Math.random() * 500, y: Math.random() * 300 },
      state: { test: 'data' },
      inputs: [],
      outputs: []
    });
  };
  
  const formatTime = (time: number): string => {
    const bars = Math.floor(time / transport.timeSignature[0]) + 1;
    const beats = Math.floor(time % transport.timeSignature[0]) + 1;
    const sixteenths = Math.floor((time % 1) * 4) + 1;
    return \`${bars}:${beats}:${sixteenths}\`;
  };
  
  return (
    <div style={{
      padding: '20px',
      background: 'linear-gradient(135deg, #667eea 0%, #764ba2 100%)',
      color: 'white',
      borderRadius: '12px',
      boxShadow: '0 4px 6px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1)',
      marginBottom: '20px'
    }}>
      <h3 style={{ marginTop: 0, marginBottom: '15px' }}>üéõÔ∏è Core Orchestrator Control</h3>
      
      <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: '1fr 1fr', gap: '20px' }}>
        {/* –õ–µ–≤–∞—è –∫–æ–ª–æ–Ω–∫–∞: –¢—Ä–∞–Ω—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç */}
        <div>
          <h4>–¢—Ä–∞–Ω—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç</h4>
          <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '10px', marginBottom: '15px' }}>
            <button 
              onClick={handleStart}
              disabled={isPlaying}
              style={{
                padding: '10px 20px',
                background: isPlaying ? '#4a5568' : '#48bb78',
                color: 'white',
                border: 'none',
                borderRadius: '6px',
                cursor: isPlaying ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer',
                fontWeight: 'bold'
              }}
            >
              ‚ñ∂Ô∏è Start
            </button>
            
            <button 
              onClick={handleStop}
              style={{
                padding: '10px 20px',
                background: '#f56565',
                color: 'white',
                border: 'none',
                borderRadius: '6px',
                cursor: 'pointer',
                fontWeight: 'bold'
              }}
            >
              ‚èπÔ∏è Stop
            </button>
            
            <button 
              onClick={handlePause}
              disabled={!isPlaying}
              style={{
                padding: '10px 20px',
                background: !isPlaying ? '#4a5568' : '#ed8936',
                color: 'white',
                border: 'none',
                borderRadius: '6px',
                cursor: !isPlaying ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer',
                fontWeight: 'bold'
              }}
            >
              ‚è∏Ô∏è Pause
            </button>
          </div>
          
          <div style={{ marginBottom: '15px' }}>
            <label style={{ display: 'block', marginBottom: '5px' }}>
              Tempo (BPM): {transport.tempo}
            </label>
            <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '10px' }}>
              <input
                type="range"
                min="40"
                max="240"
                value={tempo}
                onChange={handleTempoChange}
                style={{ flex: 1 }}
              />
              <button 
                onClick={handleTempoSubmit}
                style={{
                  padding: '5px 15px',
                  background: '#4299e1',
                  color: 'white',
                  border: 'none',
                  borderRadius: '4px',
                  cursor: 'pointer'
                }}
              >
                Set
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        {/* –ü—Ä–∞–≤–∞—è –∫–æ–ª–æ–Ω–∫–∞: –ò–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—è */}
        <div>
          <h4>–°–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏–µ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º—ã</h4>
          <div style={{ 
            background: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1)', 
            padding: '15px', 
            borderRadius: '8px',
            marginBottom: '15px'
          }}>
            <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: '1fr 1fr', gap: '10px' }}>
              <div>
                <strong>–¢–µ–∫—É—â–µ–µ –≤—Ä–µ–º—è:</strong><br />
                <span style={{ fontSize: '24px', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>
                  {formatTime(transport.currentTime)}
                </span>
              </div>
              <div>
                <strong>–†–∞–∑–º–µ—Ä —Ç–∞–∫—Ç–∞:</strong><br />
                <span style={{ fontSize: '18px' }}>
                  {transport.timeSignature[0]}/{transport.timeSignature[1]}
                </span>
              </div>
            </div>
            
            <div style={{ marginTop: '10px' }}>
              <div><strong>–ë–∞—Ä:</strong> {transport.currentBar}</div>
              <div><strong>–î–æ–ª—è:</strong> {transport.currentBeat}</div>
              <div><strong>–®–µ—Å—Ç–Ω–∞–¥—Ü–∞—Ç–∞—è:</strong> {transport.currentSixteenth}</div>
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <div>
            <strong>–ö–æ–ª–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ –Ω–æ–¥:</strong> {nodeCount}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      
      <div style={{ marginTop: '20px', paddingTop: '15px', borderTop: '1px solid rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.2)' }}>
        <button 
          onClick={handleAddTestNode}
          style={{
            padding: '8px 16px',
            background: '#9f7aea',
            color: 'white',
            border: 'none',
            borderRadius: '6px',
            cursor: 'pointer'
          }}
        >
          ‚ûï –î–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å —Ç–µ—Å—Ç–æ–≤—É—é –Ω–æ–¥—É
        </button>
        
        <button 
          onClick={() => {
            const project = coreOrchestrator.exportProject();
            console.log('üì§ Project exported:', project);
            alert('–ü—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç —ç–∫—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω –≤ –∫–æ–Ω—Å–æ–ª—å!');
          }}
          style={{
            padding: '8px 16px',
            background: '#38a169',
            color: 'white',
            border: 'none',
            borderRadius: '6px',
            cursor: 'pointer',
            marginLeft: '10px'
          }}
        >
          üíæ –≠–∫—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∞
        </button>
      </div>
      
      <div style={{ 
        marginTop: '15px', 
        fontSize: '12px', 
        opacity: 0.8,
        fontFamily: 'monospace'
      }}>
        CoreOrchestrator v0.1 | Node.js {process.versions.node} | React {React.version}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default CoreControlPanel;
EOF
```

### –®–∞–≥ 5: –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ —Ñ–∞–π–ª—ã

```
# –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä—É core –¥–∏—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∏
```

**–û–∂–∏–¥–∞–µ–º—ã–π —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç:**

- –í –¥–∏—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∏ `core` –µ—Å—Ç—å –æ–±–∞ —Ñ–∞–π–ª–∞

### –®–∞–≥ 6: –¢–µ—Å—Ç–∏—Ä—É–µ–º —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—É

–û—Ç–∫—Ä–æ–π—Ç–µ –±—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä –∏ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–π–¥–∏—Ç–µ –ø–æ –∞–¥—Ä–µ—Å—É:

1. **–î–ª—è —Ä–∞–∑—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∫–∏:**`http://localhost:5173/`
2. **–ß–µ—Ä–µ–∑ Django:**`http://localhost:8000/studio/`

**–û–∂–∏–¥–∞–µ–º—ã–π —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç:**

- –ü–æ—è–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç—Å—è –ø–∞–Ω–µ–ª—å —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è CoreOrchestrator
- –ö–Ω–æ–ø–∫–∏ Start/Stop/Pause —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—é—Ç
- –°–ª–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä —Ç–µ–º–ø–∞ –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω—è–µ—Ç BPM
- –í –∫–æ–Ω—Å–æ–ª–∏ –±—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä–∞ –≤–∏–¥–Ω—ã –ª–æ–≥–∏ —è–¥—Ä–∞
- –ö–Ω–æ–ø–∫–∞ "–î–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å —Ç–µ—Å—Ç–æ–≤—É—é –Ω–æ–¥—É" –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç –Ω–æ–¥—ã
- –ö–Ω–æ–ø–∫–∞ "–≠–∫—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∞" –ø–æ–∫–∞–∑—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –≤ –∫–æ–Ω—Å–æ–ª–∏

---

## ‚úÖ –ß—Ç–æ –º—ã —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞–ª–∏:

## üéØ –î–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ 2: –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º –±–∞–∑–æ–≤—ã–π —Ñ–∞–π–ª CoreOrchestrator.ts

### –°–º–æ—Ç—Ä–∏–º —Ç–µ–∫—É—â–µ–µ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏–µ:

(–ü–æ—Å–ª–µ –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è –î–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏—è 1)

### –ü—Ä–∏–º–µ–Ω—è–µ–º —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ:

bash

```
cat > CoreOrchestrator.ts << 'EOF'
/**
 * CoreOrchestrator - —Ü–µ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–µ —è–¥—Ä–æ —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è —Å—Ç—É–¥–∏–µ–π
 * –í–µ—Ä—Å–∏—è 0.1 - –§–∞–∑–∞ 2 (–º–µ—Å—è—Ü 3)
 */

import { EventEmitter } from 'events'

// –ë–∞–∑–æ–≤—ã–µ —Ç–∏–ø—ã –¥–ª—è —è–¥—Ä–∞
export interface TransportState {
  isPlaying: boolean
  isRecording: boolean
  currentTime: number    // –≤ beats
  tempo: number         // BPM
  timeSignature: [number, number] // [beats per bar, beat unit]
}

export interface NodeDescriptor {
  id: string
  type: string
  name: string
  position: { x: number; y: number }
}

// –û—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω–æ–π –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å —è–¥—Ä–∞
export class CoreOrchestrator extends EventEmitter {
  private transport: TransportState
  private nodes: Map<string, NodeDescriptor>
  
  constructor() {
    super()
    
    this.transport = {
      isPlaying: false,
      isRecording: false,
      currentTime: 0,
      tempo: 120,
      timeSignature: [4, 4]
    }
    
    this.nodes = new Map()
    
    console.log('üéõÔ∏è CoreOrchestrator initialized')
  }
  
  // === –¢–†–ê–ù–°–ü–û–†–¢ ===
  startTransport(): void {
    if (this.transport.isPlaying) return
    
    this.transport.isPlaying = true
    this.transport.currentTime = 0
    console.log('‚ñ∂Ô∏è Transport started')
    this.emit('transport:start', this.transport)
  }
  
  stopTransport(): void {
    this.transport.isPlaying = false
    console.log('‚èπÔ∏è Transport stopped')
    this.emit('transport:stop', this.transport)
  }
  
  setTempo(tempo: number): void {
    this.transport.tempo = Math.max(20, Math.min(300, tempo))
    console.log(\`üéµ Tempo set to ${this.transport.tempo} BPM\`)
    this.emit('tempo:change', { tempo: this.transport.tempo })
  }
  
  // === –£–ü–†–ê–í–õ–ï–ù–ò–ï –ù–û–î–ê–ú–ò ===
  addNode(node: NodeDescriptor): string {
    this.nodes.set(node.id, node)
    console.log(\`‚ûï Node added: ${node.type} (${node.id})\`)
    this.emit('node:added', { node })
    return node.id
  }
  
  removeNode(nodeId: string): boolean {
    const success = this.nodes.delete(nodeId)
    if (success) {
      console.log(\`‚ûñ Node removed: ${nodeId}\`)
      this.emit('node:removed', { nodeId })
    }
    return success
  }
  
  getNode(nodeId: string): NodeDescriptor | undefined {
    return this.nodes.get(nodeId)
  }
  
  getAllNodes(): NodeDescriptor[] {
    return Array.from(this.nodes.values())
  }
  
  // === –£–¢–ò–õ–ò–¢–´ ===
  getTransportState(): TransportState {
    return { ...this.transport }
  }
  
  reset(): void {
    this.stopTransport()
    this.nodes.clear()
    this.transport.currentTime = 0
    this.transport.tempo = 120
    console.log('üîÑ CoreOrchestrator reset')
  }
}

// –ì–ª–æ–±–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π —ç–∫–∑–µ–º–ø–ª—è—Ä —è–¥—Ä–∞
export const coreOrchestrator = new CoreOrchestrator()

export default coreOrchestrator
EOF
```

```
echo "=== –ü–µ—Ä–≤—ã–µ 10 —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫ ==="
head -10 CoreOrchestrator.ts
echo "=== –ü–æ—Å–ª–µ–¥–Ω–∏–µ 5 —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫ ==="
tail -5 CoreOrchestrator.ts
```

**–û–∂–∏–¥–∞–µ–º—ã–π —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç:**

- –§–∞–π–ª `CoreOrchestrator.ts` —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω
- –°–æ–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏—Ç ~80 —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫ –∫–æ–¥–∞
- –°–æ–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏—Ç –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å `CoreOrchestrator` –∏ —ç–∫—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç `coreOrchestrator`

**–ü–æ–¥—Ç–≤–µ—Ä–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∏–µ:** –£–∫–∞–∂–∏—Ç–µ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥.

```
      coreOrchestrator.removeAllListeners()

    coreOrchestrator.startTransport()
  }

    coreOrchestrator.stopTransport()
  }

    const newTempo = parseInt(e.target.value)
    setTempo
```

## üéØ –î–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ 3: –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º —Ä–µ–∑–µ—Ä–≤–Ω—É—é –∫–æ–ø–∏—é —Å—Ç–∞—Ä–æ–≥–æ —Ñ–∞–π–ª–∞ –∏ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º –Ω–æ–≤—É—é –≤–µ—Ä—Å–∏—é

### –°–º–æ—Ç—Ä–∏–º —Ç–µ–∫—É—â–µ–µ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏–µ:

(–ï—Å—Ç—å —Å—Ç–∞—Ä–∞—è –≤–µ—Ä—Å–∏—è CoreOrchestrator, –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–∏—Ç—å)

### –ü—Ä–∏–º–µ–Ω—è–µ–º —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ:

bash

```
echo "=== –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º —Ä–µ–∑–µ—Ä–≤–Ω—É—é –∫–æ–ø–∏—é —Å—Ç–∞—Ä–æ–≥–æ —Ñ–∞–π–ª–∞ ==="
cp CoreOrchestrator.ts CoreOrchestrator.ts.backup
echo "=== –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏–µ –±—ç–∫–∞–ø–∞ ==="
ls -la *.ts *.backup

echo "=== –ü–µ—Ä–µ–∑–∞–ø–∏—Å—ã–≤–∞–µ–º —Ñ–∞–π–ª –Ω–æ–≤–æ–π –≤–µ—Ä—Å–∏–µ–π ==="
cat > CoreOrchestrator.ts << 'EOF'
/**
 * CoreOrchestrator - —Ü–µ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–µ —è–¥—Ä–æ —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è —Å—Ç—É–¥–∏–µ–π
 * –í–µ—Ä—Å–∏—è 0.2 - –§–∞–∑–∞ 2 (–º–µ—Å—è—Ü 3), –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–æ 13.12.2025
 * 
 * –ê—Ä—Ö–∏—Ç–µ–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∞:
 * - –ï–¥–∏–Ω—ã–π —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç (play/stop/tempo)
 * - –£–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–æ–¥–∞–º–∏-—Ä–µ–¥–∞–∫—Ç–æ—Ä–∞–º–∏
 * - –°–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ —Å–æ–±—ã—Ç–∏—è EventEmitter
 */

import { EventEmitter } from 'events'

// === –¢–ò–ü–´ ===
export interface TransportState {
  isPlaying: boolean
  isRecording: boolean
  currentTime: number    // –≤ beats
  tempo: number         // BPM
  timeSignature: [number, number] // [beats per bar, beat unit]
  currentBar: number
  currentBeat: number
  currentSixteenth: number
}

export interface NodeDescriptor {
  id: string
  type: string
  name: string
  position: { x: number; y: number }
  state: Record<string, any>
  inputs: string[]
  outputs: string[]
}

export enum CoreEventType {
  TRANSPORT_START = 'transport:start',
  TRANSPORT_STOP = 'transport:stop',
  TRANSPORT_PAUSE = 'transport:pause',
  TEMPO_CHANGE = 'tempo:change',
  TIME_SIGNATURE_CHANGE = 'timesignature:change',
  NODE_ADDED = 'node:added',
  NODE_REMOVED = 'node:removed',
  NODE_CONNECTED = 'node:connected',
  NODE_DISCONNECTED = 'node:disconnected',
  CLOCK_TICK = 'clock:tick'
}

// === –û–°–ù–û–í–ù–û–ô –ö–õ–ê–°–° –Ø–î–†–ê ===
export class CoreOrchestrator extends EventEmitter {
  private transport: TransportState
  private nodes: Map<string, NodeDescriptor>
  private connections: Map<string, string[]> // sourceId -> targetId[]
  private clockInterval: NodeJS.Timeout | null
  
  constructor() {
    super()
    
    this.transport = {
      isPlaying: false,
      isRecording: false,
      currentTime: 0,
      tempo: 120,
      timeSignature: [4, 4],
      currentBar: 1,
      currentBeat: 1,
      currentSixteenth: 1
    }
    
    this.nodes = new Map()
    this.connections = new Map()
    this.clockInterval = null
    
    console.log('üéõÔ∏è CoreOrchestrator v0.2 initialized')
  }
  
  // === –¢–†–ê–ù–°–ü–û–†–¢ –ò –°–ò–ù–•–†–û–ù–ò–ó–ê–¶–ò–Ø ===
  startTransport(): void {
    if (this.transport.isPlaying) {
      console.log('‚ö†Ô∏è Transport already playing')
      return
    }
    
    this.transport.isPlaying = true
    this.transport.currentTime = 0
    this.transport.currentBar = 1
    this.transport.currentBeat = 1
    this.transport.currentSixteenth = 1
    
    // –ó–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞–µ–º –≤–Ω—É—Ç—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω–∏–µ —á–∞—Å—ã
    this.startInternalClock()
    
    this.emit(CoreEventType.TRANSPORT_START, { ...this.transport })
    console.log('‚ñ∂Ô∏è Transport started at', this.transport.tempo, 'BPM')
  }
  
  stopTransport(): void {
    this.transport.isPlaying = false
    this.stopInternalClock()
    
    this.emit(CoreEventType.TRANSPORT_STOP, { ...this.transport })
    console.log('‚èπÔ∏è Transport stopped')
  }
  
  pauseTransport(): void {
    this.transport.isPlaying = false
    this.stopInternalClock()
    
    this.emit(CoreEventType.TRANSPORT_PAUSE, { ...this.transport })
    console.log('‚è∏Ô∏è Transport paused at', this.transport.currentTime.toFixed(2), 'beats')
  }
  
  setTempo(tempo: number): void {
    const clampedTempo = Math.max(20, Math.min(300, tempo))
    this.transport.tempo = clampedTempo
    
    // –ü–µ—Ä–µ–∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞–µ–º —á–∞—Å—ã, –µ—Å–ª–∏ –æ–Ω–∏ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—é—Ç
    if (this.transport.isPlaying) {
      this.stopInternalClock()
      this.startInternalClock()
    }
    
    this.emit(CoreEventType.TEMPO_CHANGE, { tempo: this.transport.tempo })
    console.log('üéµ Tempo set to', this.transport.tempo, 'BPM')
  }
  
  setTimeSignature(numerator: number, denominator: number): void {
    this.transport.timeSignature = [numerator, denominator]
    this.emit(CoreEventType.TIME_SIGNATURE_CHANGE, { timeSignature: this.transport.timeSignature })
    console.log('üéº Time signature set to', numerator + '/' + denominator)
  }
  
  // === –£–ü–†–ê–í–õ–ï–ù–ò–ï –ù–û–î–ê–ú–ò ===
  addNode(node: NodeDescriptor): string {
    if (this.nodes.has(node.id)) {
      console.warn('‚ö†Ô∏è Node with id', node.id, 'already exists')
      return node.id
    }
    
    this.nodes.set(node.id, node)
    this.emit(CoreEventType.NODE_ADDED, { node })
    console.log('‚ûï Node added:', node.type, '(', node.id, ')')
    
    return node.id
  }
  
  removeNode(nodeId: string): boolean {
    if (!this.nodes.has(nodeId)) {
      console.warn('‚ö†Ô∏è Node not found:', nodeId)
      return false
    }
    
    const node = this.nodes.get(nodeId)!
    this.nodes.delete(nodeId)
    
    // –£–¥–∞–ª—è–µ–º –≤—Å–µ —Å–æ–µ–¥–∏–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è —Å —ç—Ç–æ–π –Ω–æ–¥–æ–π
    this.connections.delete(nodeId)
    for (const [sourceId, targets] of this.connections.entries()) {
      const newTargets = targets.filter(targetId => targetId !== nodeId)
      if (newTargets.length === 0) {
        this.connections.delete(sourceId)
      } else {
        this.connections.set(sourceId, newTargets)
      }
    }
    
    this.emit(CoreEventType.NODE_REMOVED, { nodeId })
    console.log('‚ûñ Node removed:', nodeId)
    
    return true
  }
  
  getNode(nodeId: string): NodeDescriptor | undefined {
    return this.nodes.get(nodeId)
  }
  
  getAllNodes(): NodeDescriptor[] {
    return Array.from(this.nodes.values())
  }
  
  // === –°–û–ï–î–ò–ù–ï–ù–ò–Ø –ú–ï–ñ–î–£ –ù–û–î–ê–ú–ò ===
  connectNodes(sourceId: string, targetId: string): boolean {
    if (!this.nodes.has(sourceId) || !this.nodes.has(targetId)) {
      console.warn('‚ö†Ô∏è Cannot connect: one or both nodes not found')
      return false
    }
    
    const existingConnections = this.connections.get(sourceId) || []
    if (existingConnections.includes(targetId)) {
      console.warn('‚ö†Ô∏è Connection already exists')
      return false
    }
    
    this.connections.set(sourceId, [...existingConnections, targetId])
    this.emit(CoreEventType.NODE_CONNECTED, { sourceId, targetId })
    console.log('üîó Nodes connected:', sourceId, '->', targetId)
    
    return true
  }
  
  disconnectNodes(sourceId: string, targetId: string): boolean {
    const connections = this.connections.get(sourceId)
    if (!connections || !connections.includes(targetId)) {
      console.warn('‚ö†Ô∏è Connection not found')
      return false
    }
    
    const newConnections = connections.filter(id => id !== targetId)
    if (newConnections.length === 0) {
      this.connections.delete(sourceId)
    } else {
      this.connections.set(sourceId, newConnections)
    }
    
    this.emit(CoreEventType.NODE_DISCONNECTED, { sourceId, targetId })
    console.log('üîå Nodes disconnected:', sourceId, '-/->', targetId)
    
    return true
  }
  
  // === –í–ù–£–¢–†–ï–ù–ù–ò–ï –ß–ê–°–´ ===
  private startInternalClock(): void {
    if (this.clockInterval) {
      clearInterval(this.clockInterval)
    }
    
    // –ò–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–≤–∞–ª —Ç–∏–∫–∞: 1/16 –Ω–æ—Ç—ã
    const beatsPerSecond = this.transport.tempo / 60
    const sixteenthsPerSecond = beatsPerSecond * 4
    const tickInterval = 1000 / sixteenthsPerSecond
    
    this.clockInterval = setInterval(() => {
      this.clockTick()
    }, tickInterval)
    
    console.log('‚è±Ô∏è Internal clock started, tick interval:', tickInterval.toFixed(2), 'ms')
  }
  
  private stopInternalClock(): void {
    if (this.clockInterval) {
      clearInterval(this.clockInterval)
      this.clockInterval = null
      console.log('‚è±Ô∏è Internal clock stopped')
    }
  }
  
  private clockTick(): void {
    // –û–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª—è–µ–º –≤—Ä–µ–º—è (1 —Ç–∏–∫ = 1/16 –Ω–æ—Ç—ã)
    const deltaBeats = 0.25 // 1/16 –Ω–æ—Ç—ã
    this.transport.currentTime += deltaBeats
    
    // –û–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª—è–µ–º –ø–æ–∑–∏—Ü–∏—é –≤ —Ç–∞–∫—Ç–µ
    const beatsPerBar = this.transport.timeSignature[0]
    const totalBeats = this.transport.currentTime
    
    this.transport.currentBar = Math.floor(totalBeats / beatsPerBar) + 1
    const beatsInCurrentBar = totalBeats % beatsPerBar
    this.transport.currentBeat = Math.floor(beatsInCurrentBar) + 1
    this.transport.currentSixteenth = Math.floor((beatsInCurrentBar % 1) * 4) + 1
    
    this.emit(CoreEventType.CLOCK_TICK, { ...this.transport })
  }
  
  // === –£–¢–ò–õ–ò–¢–´ ===
  getTransportState(): TransportState {
    return { ...this.transport }
  }
  
  getConnections(): Map<string, string[]> {
    return new Map(this.connections)
  }
  
  reset(): void {
    this.stopTransport()
    this.nodes.clear()
    this.connections.clear()
    this.transport.currentTime = 0
    this.transport.currentBar = 1
    this.transport.currentBeat = 1
    this.transport.currentSixteenth = 1
    console.log('üîÑ CoreOrchestrator reset')
  }
  
  exportProject(): any {
    return {
      transport: this.transport,
      nodes: Array.from(this.nodes.values()),
      connections: Array.from(this.connections.entries()),
      version: '0.2',
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    }
  }
  
  importProject(projectData: any): boolean {
    try {
      this.reset()
      
      if (projectData.transport) {
        this.transport = { ...projectData.transport }
      }
      
      if (projectData.nodes && Array.isArray(projectData.nodes)) {
        projectData.nodes.forEach((node: NodeDescriptor) => {
          this.nodes.set(node.id, node)
        })
      }
      
      if (projectData.connections && Array.isArray(projectData.connections)) {
        projectData.connections.forEach(([sourceId, targets]: [string, string[]]) => {
          this.connections.set(sourceId, targets)
        })
      }
      
      console.log('üì• Project imported:', projectData.nodes?.length || 0, 'nodes')
      return true
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('‚ùå Error importing project:', error)
      return false
    }
  }
}

// –ì–ª–æ–±–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π —ç–∫–∑–µ–º–ø–ª—è—Ä —è–¥—Ä–∞
export const coreOrchestrator = new CoreOrchestrator()

export default coreOrchestrator
EOF
```

### –¢–µ—Å—Ç–∏—Ä—É–µ–º —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç:

bash

```
echo "=== –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π —Ñ–∞–π–ª ==="
ls -lh CoreOrchestrator.ts
echo "=== –°—Ä–∞–≤–Ω–∏–≤–∞–µ–º —Ä–∞–∑–º–µ—Ä—ã ==="
echo "–ù–æ–≤—ã–π —Ñ–∞–π–ª: $(wc -l < CoreOrchestrator.ts) —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫"
echo "–°—Ç–∞—Ä—ã–π —Ñ–∞–π–ª (–±—ç–∫–∞–ø): $(wc -l < CoreOrchestrator.ts.backup) —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫"
echo "=== –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º –∫–ª—é—á–µ–≤—ã–µ —ç–∫—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç—ã ==="
grep -n "^export" CoreOrchestrator.ts | head -10
```

- –ù–æ–≤—ã–π —Ñ–∞–π–ª –±–æ–ª—å—à–µ —Å—Ç–∞—Ä–æ–≥–æ (–±–æ–ª—å—à–µ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–∞–ª–∞)
- –°–æ–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏—Ç –≤—Å–µ –Ω–µ–æ–±—Ö–æ–¥–∏–º—ã–µ —ç–∫—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç—ã: –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å, –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–π—Å—ã, enum, –≥–ª–æ–±–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π —ç–∫–∑–µ–º–ø–ª—è—Ä

**–ü–æ–¥—Ç–≤–µ—Ä–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∏–µ:** –°–æ–æ–±—â–∏—Ç–µ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥.

## üéØ –î–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ 4: –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π —Ñ–∞–π–ª

### –°–º–æ—Ç—Ä–∏–º —Ç–µ–∫—É—â–µ–µ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏–µ:

(–§–∞–π–ª –ø–µ—Ä–µ–∑–∞–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω, –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏—Ç—å —Å–æ–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏–º–æ–µ)

```

grep -n "^export" CoreOrchestrator.ts | head -10
```

**–û–∂–∏–¥–∞–µ–º—ã–π —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç:**

- –ù–æ–≤—ã–π —Ñ–∞–π–ª –∑–Ω–∞—á–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ –±–æ–ª—å—à–µ (250+ —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫ –ø—Ä–æ—Ç–∏–≤ ~40)
- –°–æ–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏—Ç –≤—Å–µ –Ω–µ–æ–±—Ö–æ–¥–∏–º—ã–µ —ç–∫—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç—ã
- –ï—Å—Ç—å –≥–ª–æ–±–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π —ç–∫–∑–µ–º–ø–ª—è—Ä `coreOrchestrator`

**–ü–æ–¥—Ç–≤–µ—Ä–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∏–µ:** –°–æ–æ–±—â–∏—Ç–µ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥.

‚úÖ **–û–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ —É—Å–ø–µ—à–Ω–æ!**

**–†–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç—ã:**

- ‚úÖ **–ù–æ–≤—ã–π —Ñ–∞–π–ª:** 9.7K, 325 —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫ (–±—ã–ª–æ 1.4K, 70 —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫)
- ‚úÖ **–í—Å–µ —ç–∫—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç—ã –ø—Ä–∏—Å—É—Ç—Å—Ç–≤—É—é—Ç:** –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–π—Å—ã, enum, –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å, –≥–ª–æ–±–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π —ç–∫–∑–µ–º–ø–ª—è—Ä
- ‚úÖ **–ì–ª–æ–±–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π —ç–∫–∑–µ–º–ø–ª—è—Ä:**`coreOrchestrator` —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –∏ —ç–∫—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç—Å—è
- ‚úÖ **–ë—ç–∫–∞–ø —Å–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–µ–Ω:**`CoreOrchestrator.ts.backup`

---

## üéØ –î–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ 5: –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–æ—Å–ø–æ—Å–æ–±–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å TypeScript –∫–æ–º–ø–∏–ª—è—Ü–∏–µ–π

### –°–º–æ—Ç—Ä–∏–º —Ç–µ–∫—É—â–µ–µ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏–µ:

(–§–∞–π–ª —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω, –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏—Ç—å —Å–∏–Ω—Ç–∞–∫—Å–∏—Å TypeScript)

### –ü—Ä–∏–º–µ–Ω—è–µ–º —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ:

bash

```
echo "=== –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º TypeScript –∫–æ–º–ø–∏–ª—è—Ü–∏—é ==="
cd /Users/kirillkravcov/UniversalCreativeHub/uch-backend/uch/apps/studio/frontend
echo "–ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º —Ç–∏–ø—ã –≤ CoreOrchestrator..."
npx tsc --noEmit --strict src/core/CoreOrchestrator.ts 2>&1 | head -20
echo "=== –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º –Ω–∞–ª–∏—á–∏–µ TypeScript –æ—à–∏–±–æ–∫ ==="
npx tsc --noEmit --strict src/core/CoreOrchestrator.ts 2>&1 | grep -i "error\|warning" | head -5
```

**–û–∂–∏–¥–∞–µ–º—ã–π —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç:**

- TypeScript –∫–æ–º–ø–∏–ª—è—Ü–∏—è –ø—Ä–æ—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç –±–µ–∑ –∫—Ä–∏—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏—Ö –æ—à–∏–±–æ–∫
- –í–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω—ã –ø—Ä–µ–¥—É–ø—Ä–µ–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∏—è, –Ω–æ –Ω–µ –æ—à–∏–±–∫–∏
- –§–∞–π–ª —Å–∏–Ω—Ç–∞–∫—Å–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏ –∫–æ—Ä—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–Ω—ã–π

**–ü–æ–¥—Ç–≤–µ—Ä–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∏–µ:** –°–æ–æ–±—â–∏—Ç–µ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥.

(venv) kirillkravcov@MacBook-Pro-Kirill core % echo "=== –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º TypeScript –∫–æ–º–ø–∏–ª—è—Ü–∏—é ===" cd /Users/kirillkravcov/UniversalCreativeHub/uch-backend/uch/apps/studio/frontend echo "–ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º —Ç–∏–ø—ã –≤ CoreOrchestrator..." npx tsc --noEmit --strict src/core/CoreOrchestrator.ts 2>&1 | head -20 echo "=== –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º –Ω–∞–ª–∏—á–∏–µ TypeScript –æ—à–∏–±–æ–∫ ===" npx tsc --noEmit --strict src/core/CoreOrchestrator.ts 2>&1 | grep -i "error\\|warning" | head -5 === –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º TypeScript –∫–æ–º–ø–∏–ª—è—Ü–∏—é === –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º —Ç–∏–ø—ã –≤ CoreOrchestrator... src/core/CoreOrchestrator.ts(157,39): error TS2802: Type 'MapIterator<\[string, string\[\]\]>' can only be iterated through when using the '--downlevelIteration' flag or with a '--target' of 'es2015' or higher. src/core/CoreOrchestrator.ts(158,41): error TS7006: Parameter 'targetId' implicitly has an 'any' type. === –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º –Ω–∞–ª–∏—á–∏–µ TypeScript –æ—à–∏–±–æ–∫ === src/core/CoreOrchestrator.ts(157,39): error TS2802: Type 'MapIterator<\[string, string\[\]\]>' can only be iterated through when using the '--downlevelIteration' flag or with a '--target' of 'es2015' or higher. src/core/CoreOrchestrator.ts(158,41): error TS7006: Parameter 'targetId' implicitly has an 'any' type.

‚úÖ **–ù–∞–π–¥–µ–Ω—ã TypeScript –æ—à–∏–±–∫–∏ (2):**

1. **–û—à–∏–±–∫–∞ TS2802:** –ü—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º–∞ —Å –∏—Ç–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–µ–π Map –≤ —Å—Ç–∞—Ä—ã—Ö –≤–µ—Ä—Å–∏—è—Ö ES
2. **–û—à–∏–±–∫–∞ TS7006:** –ù–µ—è–≤–Ω—ã–π —Ç–∏–ø –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `targetId`

## üéØ –î–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ 6: –ò—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è–µ–º TypeScript –æ—à–∏–±–∫–∏

### –°–º–æ—Ç—Ä–∏–º —Ç–µ–∫—É—â–µ–µ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏–µ:

(–ï—Å—Ç—å 2 TypeScript –æ—à–∏–±–∫–∏, –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ –∏—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å)

### –ü—Ä–∏–º–µ–Ω—è–µ–º —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ:

bash

```
echo "=== –ò—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è–µ–º –æ—à–∏–±–∫–∏ –≤ CoreOrchestrator.ts ==="

# –ò—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è–µ–º –∏—Ç–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—é Map –∏ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—è–µ–º —Ç–∏–ø—ã
cat > /tmp/fix_core.ts << 'EOF'
import { CoreOrchestrator } from './CoreOrchestrator'

// –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π —Ñ–∞–π–ª —Å –∏—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è–º–∏
EOF

# –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º –∏—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—É—é –≤–µ—Ä—Å–∏—é
cp CoreOrchestrator.ts CoreOrchestrator.ts.with_errors
cat > CoreOrchestrator.ts << 'EOF'
/**
 * CoreOrchestrator - —Ü–µ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–µ —è–¥—Ä–æ —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è —Å—Ç—É–¥–∏–µ–π
 * –í–µ—Ä—Å–∏—è 0.2 - –§–∞–∑–∞ 2 (–º–µ—Å—è—Ü 3), –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–æ 13.12.2025
 * –ò—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–æ: TypeScript –æ—à–∏–±–∫–∏ –∏—Ç–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏ Map
 */

import { EventEmitter } from 'events'

// === –¢–ò–ü–´ ===
export interface TransportState {
  isPlaying: boolean
  isRecording: boolean
  currentTime: number    // –≤ beats
  tempo: number         // BPM
  timeSignature: [number, number] // [beats per bar, beat unit]
  currentBar: number
  currentBeat: number
  currentSixteenth: number
}

export interface NodeDescriptor {
  id: string
  type: string
  name: string
  position: { x: number; y: number }
  state: Record<string, any>
  inputs: string[]
  outputs: string[]
}

export enum CoreEventType {
  TRANSPORT_START = 'transport:start',
  TRANSPORT_STOP = 'transport:stop',
  TRANSPORT_PAUSE = 'transport:pause',
  TEMPO_CHANGE = 'tempo:change',
  TIME_SIGNATURE_CHANGE = 'timesignature:change',
  NODE_ADDED = 'node:added',
  NODE_REMOVED = 'node:removed',
  NODE_CONNECTED = 'node:connected',
  NODE_DISCONNECTED = 'node:disconnected',
  CLOCK_TICK = 'clock:tick'
}

// === –û–°–ù–û–í–ù–û–ô –ö–õ–ê–°–° –Ø–î–†–ê ===
export class CoreOrchestrator extends EventEmitter {
  private transport: TransportState
  private nodes: Map<string, NodeDescriptor>
  private connections: Map<string, string[]> // sourceId -> targetId[]
  private clockInterval: NodeJS.Timeout | null
  
  constructor() {
    super()
    
    this.transport = {
      isPlaying: false,
      isRecording: false,
      currentTime: 0,
      tempo: 120,
      timeSignature: [4, 4],
      currentBar: 1,
      currentBeat: 1,
      currentSixteenth: 1
    }
    
    this.nodes = new Map()
    this.connections = new Map()
    this.clockInterval = null
    
    console.log('üéõÔ∏è CoreOrchestrator v0.2 initialized')
  }
  
  // === –¢–†–ê–ù–°–ü–û–†–¢ –ò –°–ò–ù–•–†–û–ù–ò–ó–ê–¶–ò–Ø ===
  startTransport(): void {
    if (this.transport.isPlaying) {
      console.log('‚ö†Ô∏è Transport already playing')
      return
    }
    
    this.transport.isPlaying = true
    this.transport.currentTime = 0
    this.transport.currentBar = 1
    this.transport.currentBeat = 1
    this.transport.currentSixteenth = 1
    
    // –ó–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞–µ–º –≤–Ω—É—Ç—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω–∏–µ —á–∞—Å—ã
    this.startInternalClock()
    
    this.emit(CoreEventType.TRANSPORT_START, { ...this.transport })
    console.log('‚ñ∂Ô∏è Transport started at', this.transport.tempo, 'BPM')
  }
  
  stopTransport(): void {
    this.transport.isPlaying = false
    this.stopInternalClock()
    
    this.emit(CoreEventType.TRANSPORT_STOP, { ...this.transport })
    console.log('‚èπÔ∏è Transport stopped')
  }
  
  pauseTransport(): void {
    this.transport.isPlaying = false
    this.stopInternalClock()
    
    this.emit(CoreEventType.TRANSPORT_PAUSE, { ...this.transport })
    console.log('‚è∏Ô∏è Transport paused at', this.transport.currentTime.toFixed(2), 'beats')
  }
  
  setTempo(tempo: number): void {
    const clampedTempo = Math.max(20, Math.min(300, tempo))
    this.transport.tempo = clampedTempo
    
    // –ü–µ—Ä–µ–∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞–µ–º —á–∞—Å—ã, –µ—Å–ª–∏ –æ–Ω–∏ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—é—Ç
    if (this.transport.isPlaying) {
      this.stopInternalClock()
      this.startInternalClock()
    }
    
    this.emit(CoreEventType.TEMPO_CHANGE, { tempo: this.transport.tempo })
    console.log('üéµ Tempo set to', this.transport.tempo, 'BPM')
  }
  
  setTimeSignature(numerator: number, denominator: number): void {
    this.transport.timeSignature = [numerator, denominator]
    this.emit(CoreEventType.TIME_SIGNATURE_CHANGE, { timeSignature: this.transport.timeSignature })
    console.log('üéº Time signature set to', numerator + '/' + denominator)
  }
  
  // === –£–ü–†–ê–í–õ–ï–ù–ò–ï –ù–û–î–ê–ú–ò ===
  addNode(node: NodeDescriptor): string {
    if (this.nodes.has(node.id)) {
      console.warn('‚ö†Ô∏è Node with id', node.id, 'already exists')
      return node.id
    }
    
    this.nodes.set(node.id, node)
    this.emit(CoreEventType.NODE_ADDED, { node })
    console.log('‚ûï Node added:', node.type, '(', node.id, ')')
    
    return node.id
  }
  
  removeNode(nodeId: string): boolean {
    if (!this.nodes.has(nodeId)) {
      console.warn('‚ö†Ô∏è Node not found:', nodeId)
      return false
    }
    
    const node = this.nodes.get(nodeId)!
    this.nodes.delete(nodeId)
    
    // –£–¥–∞–ª—è–µ–º –≤—Å–µ —Å–æ–µ–¥–∏–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è —Å —ç—Ç–æ–π –Ω–æ–¥–æ–π (–ò–°–ü–†–ê–í–õ–ï–ù–ù–ê–Ø –ò–¢–ï–†–ê–¶–ò–Ø)
    this.connections.delete(nodeId)
    
    // –ò—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–∞—è –∏—Ç–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è Map
    const connectionEntries = Array.from(this.connections.entries())
    for (const [sourceId, targets] of connectionEntries) {
      const newTargets = targets.filter((targetId: string) => targetId !== nodeId)
      if (newTargets.length === 0) {
        this.connections.delete(sourceId)
      } else {
        this.connections.set(sourceId, newTargets)
      }
    }
    
    this.emit(CoreEventType.NODE_REMOVED, { nodeId })
    console.log('‚ûñ Node removed:', nodeId)
    
    return true
  }
  
  getNode(nodeId: string): NodeDescriptor | undefined {
    return this.nodes.get(nodeId)
  }
  
  getAllNodes(): NodeDescriptor[] {
    return Array.from(this.nodes.values())
  }
  
  // === –°–û–ï–î–ò–ù–ï–ù–ò–Ø –ú–ï–ñ–î–£ –ù–û–î–ê–ú–ò ===
  connectNodes(sourceId: string, targetId: string): boolean {
    if (!this.nodes.has(sourceId) || !this.nodes.has(targetId)) {
      console.warn('‚ö†Ô∏è Cannot connect: one or both nodes not found')
      return false
    }
    
    const existingConnections = this.connections.get(sourceId) || []
    if (existingConnections.includes(targetId)) {
      console.warn('‚ö†Ô∏è Connection already exists')
      return false
    }
    
    this.connections.set(sourceId, [...existingConnections, targetId])
    this.emit(CoreEventType.NODE_CONNECTED, { sourceId, targetId })
    console.log('üîó Nodes connected:', sourceId, '->', targetId)
    
    return true
  }
  
  disconnectNodes(sourceId: string, targetId: string): boolean {
    const connections = this.connections.get(sourceId)
    if (!connections || !connections.includes(targetId)) {
      console.warn('‚ö†Ô∏è Connection not found')
      return false
    }
    
    const newConnections = connections.filter((id: string) => id !== targetId)
    if (newConnections.length === 0) {
      this.connections.delete(sourceId)
    } else {
      this.connections.set(sourceId, newConnections)
    }
    
    this.emit(CoreEventType.NODE_DISCONNECTED, { sourceId, targetId })
    console.log('üîå Nodes disconnected:', sourceId, '-/->', targetId)
    
    return true
  }
  
  // === –í–ù–£–¢–†–ï–ù–ù–ò–ï –ß–ê–°–´ ===
  private startInternalClock(): void {
    if (this.clockInterval) {
      clearInterval(this.clockInterval)
    }
    
    // –ò–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–≤–∞–ª —Ç–∏–∫–∞: 1/16 –Ω–æ—Ç—ã
    const beatsPerSecond = this.transport.tempo / 60
    const sixteenthsPerSecond = beatsPerSecond * 4
    const tickInterval = 1000 / sixteenthsPerSecond
    
    this.clockInterval = setInterval(() => {
      this.clockTick()
    }, tickInterval)
    
    console.log('‚è±Ô∏è Internal clock started, tick interval:', tickInterval.toFixed(2), 'ms')
  }
  
  private stopInternalClock(): void {
    if (this.clockInterval) {
      clearInterval(this.clockInterval)
      this.clockInterval = null
      console.log('‚è±Ô∏è Internal clock stopped')
    }
  }
  
  private clockTick(): void {
    // –û–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª—è–µ–º –≤—Ä–µ–º—è (1 —Ç–∏–∫ = 1/16 –Ω–æ—Ç—ã)
    const deltaBeats = 0.25 // 1/16 –Ω–æ—Ç—ã
    this.transport.currentTime += deltaBeats
    
    // –û–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª—è–µ–º –ø–æ–∑–∏—Ü–∏—é –≤ —Ç–∞–∫—Ç–µ
    const beatsPerBar = this.transport.timeSignature[0]
    const totalBeats = this.transport.currentTime
    
    this.transport.currentBar = Math.floor(totalBeats / beatsPerBar) + 1
    const beatsInCurrentBar = totalBeats % beatsPerBar
    this.transport.currentBeat = Math.floor(beatsInCurrentBar) + 1
    this.transport.currentSixteenth = Math.floor((beatsInCurrentBar % 1) * 4) + 1
    
    this.emit(CoreEventType.CLOCK_TICK, { ...this.transport })
  }
  
  // === –£–¢–ò–õ–ò–¢–´ ===
  getTransportState(): TransportState {
    return { ...this.transport }
  }
  
  getConnections(): Map<string, string[]> {
    return new Map(this.connections)
  }
  
  reset(): void {
    this.stopTransport()
    this.nodes.clear()
    this.connections.clear()
    this.transport.currentTime = 0
    this.transport.currentBar = 1
    this.transport.currentBeat = 1
    this.transport.currentSixteenth = 1
    console.log('üîÑ CoreOrchestrator reset')
  }
  
  exportProject(): any {
    return {
      transport: this.transport,
      nodes: Array.from(this.nodes.values()),
      connections: Array.from(this.connections.entries()),
      version: '0.2',
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    }
  }
  
  importProject(projectData: any): boolean {
    try {
      this.reset()
      
      if (projectData.transport) {
        this.transport = { ...projectData.transport }
      }
      
      if (projectData.nodes && Array.isArray(projectData.nodes)) {
        projectData.nodes.forEach((node: NodeDescriptor) => {
          this.nodes.set(node.id, node)
        })
      }
      
      if (projectData.connections && Array.isArray(projectData.connections)) {
        projectData.connections.forEach(([sourceId, targets]: [string, string[]]) => {
          this.connections.set(sourceId, targets)
        })
      }
      
      console.log('üì• Project imported:', projectData.nodes?.length || 0, 'nodes')
      return true
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('‚ùå Error importing project:', error)
      return false
    }
  }
}

// –ì–ª–æ–±–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π —ç–∫–∑–µ–º–ø–ª—è—Ä —è–¥—Ä–∞
export const coreOrchestrator = new CoreOrchestrator()

export default coreOrchestrator
EOF
```

### –¢–µ—Å—Ç–∏—Ä—É–µ–º —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç:

bash

```
echo "=== –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º –∏—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π —Ñ–∞–π–ª ==="
cd /Users/kirillkravcov/UniversalCreativeHub/uch-backend/uch/apps/studio/frontend
echo "–ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º TypeScript –∫–æ–º–ø–∏–ª—è—Ü–∏—é –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ –∏—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–π..."
npx tsc --noEmit --strict src/core/CoreOrchestrator.ts 2>&1 | head -10
echo "=== –°—Ä–∞–≤–Ω–∏–≤–∞–µ–º –∫–æ–ª–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ –æ—à–∏–±–æ–∫ ==="
npx tsc --noEmit --strict src/core/CoreOrchestrator.ts 2>&1 | grep -c "error"
```

**–û–∂–∏–¥–∞–µ–º—ã–π —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç:**

- TypeScript –æ—à–∏–±–∫–∏ –∏—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω—ã
- –ö–æ–º–ø–∏–ª—è—Ü–∏—è –ø—Ä–æ—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç –±–µ–∑ –æ—à–∏–±–æ–∫ (–∏–ª–∏ —Å –º–∏–Ω–∏–º–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–º–∏ –ø—Ä–µ–¥—É–ø—Ä–µ–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∏—è–º–∏)
- –ö–æ–ª–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ –æ—à–∏–±–æ–∫ = 0

**–ü–æ–¥—Ç–≤–µ—Ä–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∏–µ:** –°–æ–æ–±—â–∏—Ç–µ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥.

## üéØ –î–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ 10: –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ–π React –∫–æ–º–ø–æ–Ω–µ–Ω—Ç –¥–ª—è —Ç–µ—Å—Ç–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è CoreOrchestrator

### –°–º–æ—Ç—Ä–∏–º —Ç–µ–∫—É—â–µ–µ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏–µ:

(CoreOrchestrator —Å–∏–Ω—Ç–∞–∫—Å–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏ –∫–æ—Ä—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–µ–Ω, —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç –≤ TypeScript)

### –ü—Ä–∏–º–µ–Ω—è–µ–º —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ:

```

cd /Users/kirillkravcov/UniversalCreativeHub/uch-backend/uch/apps/studio/frontend/src/core

cat > CoreTest.tsx << 'EOF'
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { coreOrchestrator, TransportState, NodeDescriptor } from './CoreOrchestrator'

const CoreTest: React.FC = () => {
  const [transport, setTransport] = useState<TransportState>(coreOrchestrator.getTransportState())
  const [tempo, setTempo] = useState(transport.tempo)
  const [nodes, setNodes] = useState<NodeDescriptor[]>(coreOrchestrator.getAllNodes())
  
  // –ü–æ–¥–ø–∏—Å—ã–≤–∞–µ–º—Å—è –Ω–∞ —Å–æ–±—ã—Ç–∏—è —è–¥—Ä–∞
  useEffect(() => {
    const updateTransport = () => {
      setTransport(coreOrchestrator.getTransportState())
    }
    
    const updateNodes = () => {
      setNodes(coreOrchestrator.getAllNodes())
    }
    
    coreOrchestrator.on('transport:start', updateTransport)
    coreOrchestrator.on('transport:stop', updateTransport)
    coreOrchestrator.on('transport:pause', updateTransport)
    coreOrchestrator.on('tempo:change', updateTransport)
    coreOrchestrator.on('clock:tick', updateTransport)
    coreOrchestrator.on('node:added', updateNodes)
    coreOrchestrator.on('node:removed', updateNodes)
    
    return () => {
      coreOrchestrator.removeAllListeners()
    }
  }, [])
  
  const handleStart = () => {
    coreOrchestrator.startTransport()
  }
  
  const handleStop = () => {
    coreOrchestrator.stopTransport()
  }
  
  const handlePause = () => {
    coreOrchestrator.pauseTransport()
  }
  
  const handleTempoChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    const newTempo = parseInt(e.target.value)
    setTempo(newTempo)
  }
  
  const handleTempoSubmit = () => {
    coreOrchestrator.setTempo(tempo)
  }
  
  const handleAddTestNode = () => {
    const nodeId = 'test-node-' + Date.now()
    coreOrchestrator.addNode({
      id: nodeId,
      type: 'TestNode',
      name: '–¢–µ—Å—Ç–æ–≤–∞—è –Ω–æ–¥–∞',
      position: { x: Math.random() * 500, y: Math.random() * 300 },
      state: { test: 'data', random: Math.random() },
      inputs: [],
      outputs: []
    })
  }
  
  const handleRemoveNode = (nodeId: string) => {
    coreOrchestrator.removeNode(nodeId)
  }
  
  const formatTime = (time: number): string => {
    const bars = Math.floor(time / transport.timeSignature[0]) + 1
    const beats = Math.floor(time % transport.timeSignature[0]) + 1
    const sixteenths = Math.floor((time % 1) * 4) + 1
    return \`${bars}:${beats}:${sixteenths}\`
  }
  
  return (
    <div style={{
      padding: '20px',
      background: 'linear-gradient(135deg, #667eea 0%, #764ba2 100%)',
      color: 'white',
      borderRadius: '12px',
      boxShadow: '0 4px 6px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1)',
      marginBottom: '20px'
    }}>
      <h3 style={{ marginTop: 0, marginBottom: '15px' }}>üéõÔ∏è Core Orchestrator Test</h3>
      
      {/* –¢—Ä–∞–Ω—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç */}
      <div style={{ marginBottom: '20px' }}>
        <h4>–¢—Ä–∞–Ω—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç</h4>
        <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '10px', marginBottom: '10px' }}>
          <button onClick={handleStart} disabled={transport.isPlaying}
            style={{ padding: '8px 16px', background: transport.isPlaying ? '#4a5568' : '#48bb78', color: 'white', border: 'none', borderRadius: '6px', cursor: transport.isPlaying ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer' }}>
            ‚ñ∂Ô∏è Start
          </button>
          <button onClick={handleStop}
            style={{ padding: '8px 16px', background: '#f56565', color: 'white', border: 'none', borderRadius: '6px', cursor: 'pointer' }}>
            ‚èπÔ∏è Stop
          </button>
          <button onClick={handlePause} disabled={!transport.isPlaying}
            style={{ padding: '8px 16px', background: !transport.isPlaying ? '#4a5568' : '#ed8936', color: 'white', border: 'none', borderRadius: '6px', cursor: !transport.isPlaying ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer' }}>
            ‚è∏Ô∏è Pause
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div style={{ marginBottom: '10px' }}>
          <div>Tempo: {transport.tempo} BPM</div>
          <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '10px', alignItems: 'center' }}>
            <input type="range" min="40" max="240" value={tempo} onChange={handleTempoChange} style={{ flex: 1 }} />
            <button onClick={handleTempoSubmit} style={{ padding: '5px 15px', background: '#4299e1', color: 'white', border: 'none', borderRadius: '4px', cursor: 'pointer' }}>
              Set
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: '1fr 1fr', gap: '10px' }}>
          <div>
            <strong>–¢–µ–∫—É—â–µ–µ –≤—Ä–µ–º—è:</strong><br />
            <span style={{ fontSize: '20px', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>{formatTime(transport.currentTime)}</span>
          </div>
          <div>
            <strong>–†–∞–∑–º–µ—Ä —Ç–∞–∫—Ç–∞:</strong><br />
            {transport.timeSignature[0]}/{transport.timeSignature[1]}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      
      {/* –ù–æ–¥—ã */}
      <div style={{ marginBottom: '20px' }}>
        <h4>–ù–æ–¥—ã ({nodes.length})</h4>
        <button onClick={handleAddTestNode} style={{ padding: '8px 16px', background: '#9f7aea', color: 'white', border: 'none', borderRadius: '6px', cursor: 'pointer', marginBottom: '10px' }}>
          ‚ûï –î–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å —Ç–µ—Å—Ç–æ–≤—É—é –Ω–æ–¥—É
        </button>
        
        {nodes.length === 0 ? (
          <div style={{ padding: '10px', background: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1)', borderRadius: '6px' }}>
            –ù–æ–¥—ã –æ—Ç—Å—É—Ç—Å—Ç–≤—É—é—Ç
          </div>
        ) : (
          <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexWrap: 'wrap', gap: '10px' }}>
            {nodes.map(node => (
              <div key={node.id} style={{ padding: '10px', background: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1)', borderRadius: '6px', minWidth: '150px' }}>
                <div><strong>{node.name}</strong></div>
                <div style={{ fontSize: '12px', opacity: 0.8 }}>{node.type}</div>
                <div style={{ fontSize: '11px', marginTop: '5px' }}>ID: {node.id.slice(0, 8)}...</div>
                <button onClick={() => handleRemoveNode(node.id)} style={{ marginTop: '5px', padding: '3px 8px', background: '#f56565', color: 'white', border: 'none', borderRadius: '4px', cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: '12px' }}>
                  –£–¥–∞–ª–∏—Ç—å
                </button>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
      
      {/* –ò–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—è */}
      <div style={{ fontSize: '12px', opacity: 0.8, fontFamily: 'monospace', borderTop: '1px solid rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.2)', paddingTop: '10px' }}>
        CoreOrchestrator v0.2 | React {React.version} | {new Date().toLocaleTimeString()}
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

export default CoreTest
EOF
```

## üéØ –î–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ 14: –ò—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è–µ–º –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º—É —Å EventEmitter –¥–ª—è –±—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä–∞

### –°–º–æ—Ç—Ä–∏–º —Ç–µ–∫—É—â–µ–µ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏–µ:

(–û—à–∏–±–∫–∞ —Å–±–æ—Ä–∫–∏: `EventEmitter` –Ω–µ –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–µ–Ω –≤ –±—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä–µ. –ù—É–∂–Ω–∞ –±—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä–Ω–∞—è —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è.)

### –ü—Ä–∏–º–µ–Ω—è–µ–º —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ:

bash

```
echo "=== –ò—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è–µ–º EventEmitter –¥–ª—è –±—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä–∞ ==="
cd /Users/kirillkravcov/UniversalCreativeHub/uch-backend/uch/apps/studio/frontend/src/core

echo "1. –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç—É—é —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—é EventEmitter –¥–ª—è –±—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä–∞:"
cat > EventEmitter.ts << 'EOF'
/**
 * –ü—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–∞—è —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è EventEmitter –¥–ª—è –±—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä–∞
 * (–∞–ª—å—Ç–µ—Ä–Ω–∞—Ç–∏–≤–∞ Node.js events –º–æ–¥—É–ª—é)
 */
export class EventEmitter {
  private events: Map<string, Function[]> = new Map()
  
  on(event: string, listener: Function): this {
    if (!this.events.has(event)) {
      this.events.set(event, [])
    }
    this.events.get(event)!.push(listener)
    return this
  }
  
  emit(event: string, ...args: any[]): boolean {
    const listeners = this.events.get(event)
    if (!listeners || listeners.length === 0) {
      return false
    }
    
    listeners.forEach(listener => {
      try {
        listener(...args)
      } catch (error) {
        console.error(\`Error in event listener for ${event}:\`, error)
      }
    })
    
    return true
  }
  
  off(event: string, listener: Function): this {
    const listeners = this.events.get(event)
    if (!listeners) return this
    
    const index = listeners.indexOf(listener)
    if (index !== -1) {
      listeners.splice(index, 1)
    }
    
    return this
  }
  
  removeAllListeners(event?: string): this {
    if (event) {
      this.events.delete(event)
    } else {
      this.events.clear()
    }
    return this
  }
  
  once(event: string, listener: Function): this {
    const onceWrapper = (...args: any[]) => {
      this.off(event, onceWrapper)
      listener(...args)
    }
    return this.on(event, onceWrapper)
  }
  
  listenerCount(event: string): number {
    const listeners = this.events.get(event)
    return listeners ? listeners.length : 0
  }
}
EOF

echo "2. –û–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª—è–µ–º CoreOrchestrator –¥–ª—è –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è –Ω–∞—à–µ–π —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏:"
# –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π —Ñ–∞–π–ª —Å –∏—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è–º–∏
cp CoreOrchestrator.ts CoreOrchestrator.ts.pre_fix

# –ò—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–µ–º –Ω–∞—à—É EventEmitter –≤–º–µ—Å—Ç–æ Node.js –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è
sed -i '' '11s/import { EventEmitter } from "events"/import { EventEmitter } from ".\/EventEmitter"/' CoreOrchestrator.ts

echo "3. –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º –∏—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ:"
grep -n "import.*EventEmitter" CoreOrchestrator.ts
echo "=== –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ–º –Ω–∞–ª–∏—á–∏–µ —Ñ–∞–π–ª–∞ EventEmitter.ts ==="
ls -la EventEmitter.ts
```

**–û–∂–∏–¥–∞–µ–º—ã–π —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç:**

–í–∏–∂—É –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º—É - –Ω–µ–∑–∞–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–Ω–∞—è –∫–æ–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ü–∏—è `if`. –î–∞–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏–º –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥—ã –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–ª—å–Ω–æ:

2. **TypeScript –æ—à–∏–±–∫–∏ –∏—Ç–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏ Map:**
	- **–ü—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º–∞:**`for (const [key, value] of map.entries())` —Ç—Ä–µ–±—É–µ—Ç ES2015+
	- **–†–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ:** –ò—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ `Array.from(map.entries())`
3. **–ò–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è Vite + Django:**
	- **–†–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ:** –î–≤–∞ —Ä–µ–∂–∏–º–∞:
